			  echo gdb | sed -e "$t"` ; \
		if test "x$transformed_name" = x; then \
		  transformed_name=gdb ; \
		else \
		  true ; \
		fi ; \
		/bin/bash ./../mkinstalldirs /media/tuochenvm/ubuntu_ext/git/tuochenlyu/openwrt/build_dir/target-mips_34kc_uClibc-0.9.33.2/gdb-7.5/ipkg-install/usr/bin ; \
